<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.
//There are two 64 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 64 bit value, [63:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_64(output [63:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [63:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [63:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

  adder_32 adder_32_1(.sum(sum_temp[31:0]),
                      .cout(cout_temp),
                      .in1(in1[31:0]),
                      .in2(in2[31:0]),
                      .cin(cin));

  adder_32 adder_32_2(.sum(sum_temp[63:32]),
                      .cout(),
                      .in1(in1[63:32]),
                      .in2(in2[63:32]),
                      .cin(cout_temp));

endmodule

<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.

<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.
//There are two 64 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 64 bit value, [63:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_64(output [63:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [63:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [63:0] sum_wire;
  wire cout_wire;

  assign sum = sum_wire;
  assign cout = cout_wire;

  //Adding two 32-bit numbers

<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.
//There are two 64 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 64 bit value, [63:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_64(output [63:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [63:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [63:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[63] & in2[63]) ^ (in1[63] & sum_temp[63]) ^ (in2[63] & sum_temp[63]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.
//There are two 64 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 64 bit value, [63:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_64(output [63:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [63:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [63:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[63] & in2[63]) ^ (in1[63] & sum_temp[63]) ^ (in2[63] & sum_temp[63]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.
//There are two 64 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 64 bit value, [63:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_64(output [63:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [63:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [63:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[63] & in2[63]) ^ (in1[63] & sum_temp[63]) ^ (in2[63] & sum_temp[63]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.
//There are two 64 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 64 bit value, [63:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_64(output [63:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [63:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [63:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[63] & in2[63]) ^ (in1[63] & sum_temp[63]) ^ (in2[63] & sum_temp[63]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.
//There are two 64 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 64 bit value, [63:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_64(output [63:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [63:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [63:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[63] & in2[63]) ^ (in1[63] & sum_temp[63]) ^ (in2[63] & sum_temp[63]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.
//There are two 64 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 64 bit value, [63:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_64(output [63:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [63:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [63:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.
//There are two 64 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 64 bit value, [63:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_64(output [63:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [63:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [63:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[63] & in2[63]) ^ (in1[63] & sum_temp[63]) ^ (in2[63] & sum_temp[63]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.
//There are two 64 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 64 bit value, [63:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_64(output [63:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [63:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [63:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[63] & in2[63]) ^ (in1[63] & sum_temp[63]) ^ (in2[63] & sum_temp[63]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.

//The outputs are a 64 bit value, [63:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.

<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.
//There are two 64 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 64 bit value, [63:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.

                      output cout,

<s> //Design a 64-bit adder.
//There are two 64 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 64 bit value, [63:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_64(output [63:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [63:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin);
